endfunction
function tp takes nothing returns nothing
local integer tP=1
local integer tq=(4+(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A06R',GetTriggerUnit())*2))
loop
exitwhen tP>tq
call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e00C',GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()),bj_UNIT_FACING)
call GroupAddUnit(Ae,bj_lastCreatedUnit)
call ShowUnitHide(bj_lastCreatedUnit)
call UnitAddAbility(bj_lastCreatedUnit,'A07L')
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07L',bj_lastCreatedUnit,tP)
call IssueImmediateOrderById(bj_lastCreatedUnit,852096)
call TriggerSleepAction(0.05)
call TerrainDeformationRippleBJ(0.03,false,GetUnitLoc(bj_lastCreatedUnit),(150.00+(100.00*I2R(tP))),(150.00+(100.00*I2R(tP))),72.00,0.03,512)
set tP=tP+1
endloop
call TriggerSleepAction(2)
call ForGroupBJ(Ae,function tO)
endfunction

function tr takes nothing returns nothing
local unit tR
set tR=CreateUnit(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),'e00Q',GetUnitX(GetTriggerUnit()),GetUnitY(GetTriggerUnit()),bj_UNIT_FACING)
call SetUnitPathing(tR,false)
call SetUnitInvulnerable(tR,true)
call UnitAddAbility(tR,'Aloc')
call UnitAddAbility(tR,'A0HN')
call UnitAddAbility(tR,'A0HM')
call UnitAddAbility(tR,'A0HO')
call PolledWait(0.25)
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0HN',tR,GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0H0',GetTriggerUnit()))
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0HM',tR,GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0H0',GetTriggerUnit()))
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0HO',tR,GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0H0',GetTriggerUnit()))
call IssueImmediateOrderById(tR,852177)
call IssueImmediateOrderById(tR,852556)
call IssueTargetOrderById(tR,852069,GetTriggerUnit())
set tR=null
endfunction

function tV takes nothing returns nothing
local location FH
loop
exitwhen IsUnitDeadBJ(GetTriggerUnit())
set FH=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('B04U',EFFECT_TYPE_TARGET,FH))
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('B04T',EFFECT_TYPE_TARGET,FH))
call RemoveLocation(FH)
call PolledWait(1.50)
set FH=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('B04U',EFFECT_TYPE_TARGET,FH))
call RemoveLocation(FH)
call PolledWait(1.50)
set FH=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('B04U',EFFECT_TYPE_TARGET,FH))
call RemoveLocation(FH)
call PolledWait(1.50)
set FH=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('B04U',EFFECT_TYPE_TARGET,FH))
call RemoveLocation(FH)
endloop
set FH=null
endfunction
function tw takes nothing returns boolean
if (not (GetSpellAbilityId()=='A0G4')) then
return false
endif
return true
endfunction
function tW takes nothing returns nothing
if(GetEventDamageSource()==bC) then
call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
call UnitDamageTargetBJ(bC,GetTriggerUnit(),100*I2R(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0G4',bC)),ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL,DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
endif
endfunction
function tx takes nothing returns nothing
local timer t=GetExpiredTimer()
local real tX=fz(t,"fadeout")
call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(bC,100,100,100,tX)
if tX!=100 then
set tX=tX+10
call fX(t,"fadeout",tX)
endif
endfunction
function ty takes nothing returns nothing
local timer t=GetExpiredTimer()
local real tX=fz(t,"fadeout")
call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(bC,100,100,100,tX)
if tX!=0 then
set tX=tX-1
call fX(t,"fadeout",tX)
endif
endfunction
function tY takes nothing returns nothing
local unit ol=GetTriggerUnit()
local unit oL=GetSpellTargetUnit()
local real tz=1
local trigger sp=CreateTrigger()
local timer t=CreateTimer()
set bC=ol
call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(ol,35)
call fX(t,"fadeout",tz)
call TimerStart(t,0.01,true,function tx)
call TriggerSleepAction(1)
set bd=oL
call SetUnitPositionLocFacingLocBJ(ol,PolarProjectionBJ(GetUnitLoc(oL),80.00,AngleBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(ol),GetUnitLoc(oL))),GetUnitLoc(oL))
call PauseTimer(t)
call fZ(t)
call DestroyTimer(t)
set t=CreateTimer()
call fX(t,"fadeout",100)
call EnableTrigger(e3)
set bD=true
call SetUnitAnimation(ol,"attack")
call IssueTargetOrderById(ol,851983,oL)
call TriggerRegisterUnitEvent(sp,oL,EVENT_UNIT_DAMAGED)
call TriggerAddAction(sp,function tW)
call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(ol,100.00)
call TriggerSleepAction(0.5)
call TimerStart(t,0.01,true,function ty)
call PauseTimer(t)
call fZ(t)
call DestroyTimer(t)
call DestroyTrigger(sp)
call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(bC,100,100,100,0)
endfunction
function tZ takes nothing returns boolean
if (not (GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0ES',GetAttacker())>0)) then
return false
endif
if (IsUnitAlly(GetTriggerUnit(),GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()))) then
return false
endif
return true
endfunction
function t0 takes nothing returns nothing
local real t1=GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetAttacker())*0.04*GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0ES',GetAttacker())
call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
call UnitDamageTargetBJ(GetAttacker(),GetTriggerUnit(),t1,ATTACK_TYPE_CHAOS,DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
call TriggerSleepAction(0.70)
call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction
constant function t2 takes real Fg returns real
return 0+Fg*20
endfunction
constant function t3 takes real Fg returns real
return 5+Fg*0
endfunction
constant function t4 takes real Fg returns real
return 0.01+Fg*0.01
endfunction
constant function t5 takes real Fg returns real
return 0.2+Fg*0.1
endfunction
constant function t6 takes real Fg returns real
return 0.98
endfunction
constant function t7 takes real Fg returns real
return 0+Fg*0
endfunction
function t8 takes nothing returns boolean
if (not (GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0G5',GetAttacker())>0 and IsUnitIllusion(GetAttacker())==false)) then
return false
endif
if (not (IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE)==false)) then
return false
endif
if (GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit())=='n00L') then
return false
endif
if (IsUnitAlly(GetTriggerUnit(),GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()))) then
return false
endif
if (bD)then
set bD=false
return true
endif
if(GetRandomInt(1,100)>17) then
return false
endif
return true
endfunction
function t9 takes timer t returns unit
return fy(t,"target")
endfunction
function Ta takes timer t returns unit
return fy(t,"caster")
endfunction
function TA takes timer t returns real
return fz(t,"angle")
endfunction
function Tb takes nothing returns boolean
return (IsDestructableAliveBJ(GetEnumDestructable()))
endfunction
function TB takes nothing returns nothing
if (Tb()) then
set bj_randomSubGroupWant=bj_randomSubGroupWant+1
endif
endfunction
function Tc takes location TC,real Td returns integer
local integer TD=bj_randomSubGroupWant
local integer Te
set bj_randomSubGroupWant=0
call EnumDestructablesInCircleBJ(Td,TC,function TB)
set Te=bj_randomSubGroupWant
set bj_randomSubGroupWant=TD
return Te
endfunction
function TE takes nothing returns nothing
call KillDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
endfunction
function Tf takes unit TF returns real
return fz(TF,"movement")
endfunction
function Tg takes nothing returns nothing
local timer t=GetExpiredTimer()
local unit oL=t9(t)
local unit ol=Ta(t)
local unit TF=t9(t)
local real TG=TA(t)
local integer Fg=fY(t,"level")
local real Th=Tf(TF)
local location TH=GetUnitLoc(oL)
local location Ti=Location(GetUnitX(oL)+Th*CosBJ(TG),GetUnitY(oL)+Th*SinBJ(TG))
local integer TI=0
local integer Tj=fY(t,"brake")
if Tj==1 then
set Th=Tf(TF)
set Th=Th*t6(Fg)
call fX(TF,"movement",Th)
endif
set TI=Tc(TH,150)
call UnitDamageTargetBJ(ol,oL,(0.5+I2R(TI)*t7(Fg)),ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL,DAMAGE_TYPE_UNKNOWN)
call EnumDestructablesInCircleBJ(150.00,TH,function TE)
call DestroyEffect(AddSpellEffectByIdLoc('A0G5',EFFECT_TYPE_SPECIAL,TH))
call RemoveLocation(TH)
call SetUnitPositionLoc(oL,Ti)
call RemoveLocation(Ti)
set t=null
set oL=null
set TH=null
set Ti=null
set ol=null
set TF=null
set TI=0
endfunction
function TJ takes nothing returns nothing
local unit oL=GetTriggerUnit()
local unit ol=GetAttacker()
local unit TF=GetTriggerUnit()
local location a=GetUnitLoc(ol)
local location b=GetUnitLoc(oL)
local real TG=AngleBetweenPoints(a,b)
local timer t=CreateTimer()
local integer Fg=GetUnitAbilityLevel(ol,'A0G5')
local real Th=t3(Fg)
local integer Tj=0
local effect fx=AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("weapon",ol,"Abilities\\Weapons\\PhoenixMissile\\Phoenix_Missile_mini.mdl")
call DestroyEffect(fx)
call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
call RemoveLocation(b)
call fU(t,"target",oL)
call fU(t,"caster",ol)
call fX(t,"angle",TG)
call fW(t,"level",Fg)
call fX(t,"movement",Fg)
call fX(TF,"movement",Th)
call UnitDamageTargetBJ(ol,oL,t2(Fg),ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL,DAMAGE_TYPE_UNKNOWN)
call TimerStart(t,0.01,true,function Tg)
call PolledWait(t4(Fg))
set Tj=1
call fW(t,"brake",Tj)
call PolledWait(t5(I2R(Fg)))
call fZ(t)
call fZ(TF)
call DestroyTimer(t)
call IssuePointOrderByIdLoc(oL,851990,a)
call RemoveLocation(a)
set oL=null
set ol=null
set a=null
set b=null
set t=null
set TF=null
call TriggerSleepAction(1.5)
call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

function TK takes nothing returns nothing
local integer Tl=GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0GJ',GetTriggerUnit())

set aX=GetTriggerUnit()
set aY=GetSpellTargetUnit()
call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e00C',GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()),bj_UNIT_FACING)
set az=bj_lastCreatedUnit
call SetUnitPathing(az,false)
call UnitAddAbility(az,'Aloc')
call SetUnitInvulnerable(az,true)
if (Tl==1) then
call UnitAddAbility(az,'A0GE')
set aZ='A0GE'
elseif (Tl==2) then
call UnitAddAbility(az,'A0GF')
set aZ='A0GF'
elseif (Tl==3) then
call UnitAddAbility(az,'A0GG')
set aZ='A0GG'
elseif (Tl==4) then
call UnitAddAbility(az,'A0GH')
set aZ='A0GH'
endif
call IssueTargetOrderById(GetTriggerUnit(),851983,GetSpellTargetUnit())
call TriggerSleepAction(0.01)
call SetUnitPathing(GetTriggerUnit(),false)
call EnableTrigger(e6)
call EnableTrigger(e5)
call EnableTrigger(e8)
call EnableTrigger(e7)
endfunction

call UnitRemoveAbility(aY,'B01Y')

function TY takes nothing returns boolean

function TZ takes nothing returns nothing
local integer T0
local integer Gq
local integer GQ
local integer T1=200
local real array PN
local unit array T2
local unit T3=GetTriggerUnit()
local unit nn
local location T4=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
local location T5
local location T6
local group T7
if (GetSpellAbilityId()=='A013') then
set T0=GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A013',GetTriggerUnit())
else
set T0=(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0A6',GetTriggerUnit())+1)
endif
set Gq=1
set GQ=18
loop
exitwhen Gq>GQ
set T5=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e017',GetOwningPlayer(T3),T5,PN[Gq])
if (GetSpellAbilityId()=='A013') then
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A057',bj_lastCreatedUnit,GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A013',GetSpellAbilityUnit()))
else
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A057',bj_lastCreatedUnit,(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A0A6',GetSpellAbilityUnit())+1))
endif
set T2[Gq]=bj_lastCreatedUnit
call IssuePointOrderByIdLoc(bj_lastCreatedUnit,851986,PolarProjectionBJ(T5,675.00,(I2R(Gq)*20.00)))
call RemoveLocation(T5)
set Gq=Gq+1
endloop
set Gq=1
set GQ=5
loop
exitwhen Gq>GQ
set T7=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(T1,T4,Condition(function TY))
loop
set nn=FirstOfGroup(T7)
exitwhen nn==null
set T6=GetUnitLoc(nn)
call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'o00I',GetOwningPlayer(T3),T6,bj_UNIT_FACING)
call UnitAddAbility(bj_lastCreatedUnit,'A076')
call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A076',bj_lastCreatedUnit,T0)
call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(1.00,'BTLF',bj_lastCreatedUnit)
call IssueTargetOrderById(bj_lastCreatedUnit,851983,nn)
call SetUnitPathing(bj_lastCreatedUnit,false)
call SetUnitInvulnerable(bj_lastCreatedUnit,true)
call UnitAddAbility(bj_lastCreatedUnit,'Aloc')
call RemoveLocation(T6)
call GroupRemoveUnit(T7,nn)
endloop
set T1=T1+200
call TriggerSleepAction(0.18)
set Gq=Gq+1
endloop
set Gq=1
set GQ=18
loop
exitwhen Gq>GQ
call RemoveUnit(T2[Gq])
set Gq=Gq+1
endloop
call RemoveLocation(T4)
call RemoveLocation(T5)
call DestroyGroup(T7)
set T4=null
set T5=null
set T7=null
set T6=null
endfunction
